REASONING.batch.2.d — deepseek_v4
Normal text around reasoning
Input:
input_text="before <think>thinking</think> after"
Dynamo:
reasoning_text="thinking"
normal_text="before  after"
vLLM:
reasoning_text="thinking"
normal_text=" after"
SGLang:
reasoning_text="before thinking"
normal_text=" after"
Explanations:
vLLM: Dynamo keeps visible text outside a complete reasoning span as normal_text; vLLM drops the prefix.
SGLang: Dynamo keeps text emitted before the reasoning open marker as normal_text; SGLang strips the start marker in place and folds that prefix into reasoning_text.
Harness flags:

REASONING.batch.3.b — deepseek_v4
Open reasoning interrupted by downstream tool-call text is not configured for DeepSeek V4
Why n/a:
Dynamo's DeepSeek V4 reasoning parser has no downstream tool-call boundary while reasoning is open; closed-span handoff is covered by REASONING.batch.3.a.

REASONING.batch.3.c — deepseek_v4
Recipientless Harmony commentary is not applicable to DeepSeek V4

DeepSeek V4 does not use Harmony commentary channels; visible text and downstream tool handoff use DeepSeek-specific think and DSML tool-call markers.

REASONING.batch.3.d — deepseek_v4
Directed Harmony commentary tool calls are not applicable to DeepSeek V4

n/a
REASONING.batch.3.e — deepseek_v4
Directed Harmony analysis tool calls are not applicable to DeepSeek V4
Why n/a:
DeepSeek V4 does not use Harmony `analysis to=functions.*` envelopes; reasoning is represented by think tags.
n/a
REASONING.batch.3.f — deepseek_v4
Harmony analysis/commentary/final channel sequencing is not applicable to DeepSeek V4
Why n/a:
DeepSeek V4 has no Harmony channel protocol, so mixed analysis, commentary tool call, and final-channel sequencing is outside its grammar.

REASONING.batch.4 — deepseek_v4
Dangling end marker without an opening think tag
Input:
input_text="normal</think>answer"
Dynamo:
reasoning_text="normal"
normal_text="answer"
vLLM:
reasoning_text="normal"
normal_text="answer"
SGLang:
reasoning_text=""
normal_text="normal</think>answer"
Explanations:
SGLang: Dynamo treats the text before an unpaired end marker as reasoning (implicit-opener recovery, matching vLLM); SGLang enters reasoning only on an explicit start marker, so the dangling end marker and surrounding text stay in normal_text.

REASONING.batch.6.a — deepseek_v4
Multiple reasoning spans are concatenated by Dynamo
Input:
input_text="<think>first</think> middle <think>second</think> done"
Dynamo:
reasoning_text="firstsecond"
normal_text="middle  done"
vLLM:
reasoning_text="first"
normal_text=" middle <think>second</think> done"
SGLang:
reasoning_text="first"
normal_text=" middle <think>second</think> done"
Explanations:
vLLM: Dynamo extracts each complete reasoning span; vLLM leaves the later complete span in normal_text.
SGLang: Dynamo extracts every complete reasoning span and concatenates them; SGLang exits reasoning at the first end marker and leaves the later span, with its literal markers, in normal_text.
Harness flags:
Parity harness flags used for this result:
dynamo: parser_family=deepseek_v4; in_reasoning=false; token_ids=none
vllm: reasoning_parser=deepseek_v4; chat_template_kwargs={"enable_thinking": true}; request.skip_special_tokens=false
sglang: model_type=deepseek-v4; stream_reasoning=true; force_reasoning=false

Not set by this parser-level parity harness:
- frontend `tool_choice`
- SGLang `separate_reasoning`
- request `enable_thinking` / `thinking` / `thinking_mode` unless shown in vLLM chat_template_kwargs above
Ref:
inspired by vLLM DeepSeek V4 alias coverage in DeepSeek V3 reasoning tests: https://github.com/vllm-project/vllm/blob/39910f2b25aacc09f5e7f166cdf0030b19f8b9e8/tests/reasoning/test_deepseekv3_reasoning_parser.py; local taxonomy: lib/parsers/REASONING_CASES.md

Why n/a:
Gemma 4 has no Harmony channel protocol, so mixed analysis, commentary tool call, and final-channel sequencing is outside its grammar.

REASONING.batch.4 — gemma4
Dangling Gemma channel end marker extracts text before the marker as reasoning
Input:
input_text="normal<channel|>answer"
Dynamo:
reasoning_text="normal"
normal_text="answer"
vLLM:
reasoning_text="normal"
normal_text="answer"
SGLang:
reasoning_text=""
normal_text="normal<channel|>answer"
Explanations:
SGLang: Dynamo treats the text before an unpaired end marker as reasoning (implicit-opener recovery, matching vLLM); SGLang enters reasoning only on an explicit start marker, so the dangling end marker and surrounding text stay in normal_text.
Harness flags:

REASONING.batch.5 — gemma4
Open thought channel without close treats suffix as reasoning
Input:
input_text="intro <|channel>thought
partial"
Dynamo:
reasoning_text="partial"
normal_text="intro "
vLLM:
reasoning_text="partial"
normal_text=""
SGLang:
reasoning_text="intro partial"
normal_text=""
Explanations:
vLLM: vLLM drops text before an open Gemma reasoning channel.
SGLang: Dynamo keeps text before an unclosed reasoning channel as normal_text and the channel body as reasoning; SGLang strips the open marker in place and folds the entire prefix into reasoning_text.

- SGLang `separate_reasoning`

inspired by vLLM Gemma4 reasoning tests: https://github.com/vllm-project/vllm/blob/39910f2b25aacc09f5e7f166cdf0030b19f8b9e8/tests/reasoning/test_gemma4_reasoning_parser.py; local taxonomy: lib/parsers/REASONING_CASES.md

REASONING.batch.6.a — gemma4
Multiple reasoning spans are concatenated by Dynamo
Input:
input_text="<|channel>thought
first<channel|> middle <|channel>thought
second<channel|> done"
Dynamo:
reasoning_text="firstsecond"
normal_text=" middle  done"
vLLM:
reasoning_text="first"
normal_text=" middle <|channel>thought
second<channel|> done"
SGLang:
reasoning_text="first"
normal_text=" middle <|channel>thought
second<channel|> done"
Explanations:
vLLM: Multi-span reasoning is out-of-spec model output; Dynamo preserves all reasoning and non-reasoning text without leaking protocol markers, while vLLM leaves the later complete channel in normal_text.
SGLang: Dynamo extracts every complete reasoning span and concatenates them; SGLang exits reasoning at the first end marker and leaves the later span, with its literal markers, in normal_text.
Harness flags:
Parity harness flags used for this result:
dynamo: parser_family=gemma4; in_reasoning=false; token_ids=none
vllm: reasoning_parser=gemma4; chat_template_kwargs={}; request.skip_special_tokens=false
sglang: model_type=gemma4; stream_reasoning=true; force_reasoning=false

Not set by this parser-level parity harness:
- frontend `tool_choice`
- SGLang `separate_reasoning`
- request `enable_thinking` / `thinking` / `thinking_mode` unless shown in vLLM chat_template_kwargs above
Ref:
inspired by vLLM Gemma4 reasoning tests: https://github.com/vllm-project/vllm/blob/39910f2b25aacc09f5e7f166cdf0030b19f8b9e8/tests/reasoning/test_gemma4_reasoning_parser.py; local taxonomy: lib/parsers/REASONING_CASES.md
Spec ref:
lib/parsers/REASONING_CASES.md; https://docs.vllm.ai/en/v0.21.0/api/vllm/reasoning/gemma4_reasoning_parser/; https://docs.nvidia.com/dynamo/dev/user-guides/reasoning/reasoning-parsing-dynamo

REASONING.batch.6.a — glm45
Multiple reasoning spans are concatenated by Dynamo
Input:
input_text="<think>first</think> middle <think>second</think> done"
Dynamo:
reasoning_text="firstsecond"
normal_text="middle  done"
vLLM:
reasoning_text="first"
normal_text=" middle <think>second</think> done"
SGLang:
reasoning_text="first"
normal_text=" middle <think>second</think> done"
Family mapping:
This row uses the public GLM/Nemotron reasoning parser family 'glm45'; fixtures are shared with 'nemotron_deci' because GLM and Nemotron use the same parser implementation here.
Explanations:
vLLM: Dynamo extracts each complete reasoning span; vLLM leaves the later complete span in normal_text.
SGLang: Dynamo extracts every complete reasoning span and concatenates them; SGLang exits reasoning at the first end marker and leaves the later span, with its literal markers, in normal_text.
Harness flags:
Parity harness flags used for this result:
dynamo: parser_family=glm45; fixture_family=nemotron_deci; in_reasoning=false; token_ids=none
vllm: reasoning_parser=glm45; chat_template_kwargs={}; request.skip_special_tokens=false
sglang: model_type=glm45; stream_reasoning=true; force_reasoning=false

Not set by this parser-level parity harness:
- frontend `tool_choice`
- SGLang `separate_reasoning`
- request `enable_thinking` / `thinking` / `thinking_mode` unless shown in vLLM chat_template_kwargs above
Ref:
inspired by vLLM GLM/Nemotron think-tag reasoning tests: https://github.com/vllm-project/vllm/blob/39910f2b25aacc09f5e7f166cdf0030b19f8b9e8/tests/reasoning/test_glm4_moe_reasoning_parser.py and https://github.com/vllm-project/vllm/blob/39910f2b25aacc09f5e7f166cdf0030b19f8b9e8/tests/reasoning/test_nemotron_v3_reasoning_parser.py; local taxonomy: lib/parsers/REASONING_CASES.md

REASONING.batch.3.a — gpt_oss
Harmony analysis followed by commentary tool-call channel
Input:
input_text="<|channel|>analysis<|message|>choose tool<|end|><|start|>assistant<|channel|>commentary to=functions.get_weather <|constrain|>json<|message|>{"city":"SF"}<|call|>"
Dynamo:
reasoning_text="choose tool"
normal_text="<|start|>assistant<|channel|>commentary to=functions.get_weather <|constrain|>json<|message|>{"city":"SF"}<|call|>"
vLLM:
reasoning_text="choose tool"
normal_text=""
SGLang:
reasoning_text="choose tool"
normal_text="<|start|>assistant<|channel|>commentary to=functions.get_weather <|constrain|>json<|message|>{"city":"SF"}<|call|>"
Explanations:
vLLM: vLLM batch reasoning suppresses directed Harmony commentary at the reasoning layer; Dynamo keeps it because normal_text is the handoff to the Harmony tool parser.
Dynamo: Unlike vLLM batch reasoning, Dynamo parses reasoning before tool calling. For GPT-OSS/Harmony, directed commentary is tool-call text, so Dynamo passes it in normal_text for the Harmony tool parser to emit structured tool_calls and remove the markup from final content.
Harness flags:
Parity harness flags used for this result:
dynamo: parser_family=gpt_oss; in_reasoning=false; token_ids=none
vllm: reasoning_parser=openai_gptoss; chat_template_kwargs={}; request.skip_special_tokens=false
sglang: model_type=gpt-oss; stream_reasoning=true; force_reasoning=false

Not set by this parser-level parity harness:
- frontend `tool_choice`
- SGLang `separate_reasoning`
- request `enable_thinking` / `thinking` / `thinking_mode` unless shown in vLLM chat_template_kwargs above
Ref:
inspired by vLLM GPT-OSS reasoning tests: https://github.com/vllm-project/vllm/blob/39910f2b25aacc09f5e7f166cdf0030b19f8b9e8/tests/reasoning/test_gptoss_reasoning_parser.py; local taxonomy: lib/parsers/REASONING_CASES.md

REASONING.batch.3.e — gpt_oss
Directed Harmony analysis tool call stays in reasoning text
Input:
input_text="<|channel|>analysis to=functions.search <|constrain|>json<|message|>{"q":"x"}<|call|>"
Dynamo:
reasoning_text="{"q":"x"}"
normal_text=""
vLLM:
reasoning_text="{"q":"x"}"
normal_text=""
SGLang:
reasoning_text=""
normal_text="<|channel|>analysis to=functions.search <|constrain|>json<|message|>{"q":"x"}<|call|>"
Explanations:
SGLang: SGLang classifies a directed Harmony analysis channel ending in <|call|> as a tool_call handoff and emits the raw envelope in normal_text; Dynamo/vLLM keep analysis-channel payload hidden in reasoning_text for this parser-level contract.
Dynamo: Unlike SGLang, Dynamo only passes GPT-OSS/Harmony function calls from commentary to=functions.* to the tool-call parser. This analysis to=functions.search block is reasoning-channel text, so Dynamo keeps its payload in reasoning_text.
Harness flags:
Parity harness flags used for this result:
dynamo: parser_family=gpt_oss; in_reasoning=false; token_ids=none
vllm: reasoning_parser=openai_gptoss; chat_template_kwargs={}; request.skip_special_tokens=false
sglang: model_type=gpt-oss; stream_reasoning=true; force_reasoning=false

REASONING.batch.3.f — gpt_oss
Harmony analysis, directed commentary tool call, then final answer
Input:
input_text="<|channel|>analysis<|message|>think<|end|><|start|>assistant<|channel|>commentary to=functions.get_weather <|constrain|>json<|message|>{"city":"SF"}<|call|><|start|>assistant<|channel|>final<|message|>It is sunny."
Dynamo:
reasoning_text="think"
normal_text="<|start|>assistant<|channel|>commentary to=functions.get_weather <|constrain|>json<|message|>{"city":"SF"}<|call|><|start|>assistant<|channel|>final<|message|>It is sunny."
vLLM:
reasoning_text="think"
normal_text="It is sunny."
SGLang:
reasoning_text="think"
normal_text="<|start|>assistant<|channel|>commentary to=functions.get_weather <|constrain|>json<|message|>{"city":"SF"}<|call|>It is sunny."
Explanations:
vLLM: vLLM batch reasoning suppresses directed Harmony commentary at the reasoning layer; Dynamo keeps it because normal_text is the handoff to the Harmony tool parser.
SGLang: SGLang preserves directed Harmony commentary for downstream parsing but strips the final-channel envelope before returning normal_text; Dynamo keeps the final Harmony envelope too so the downstream Harmony tool parser can recover final text after extracting the call.
Dynamo: Unlike vLLM batch reasoning, Dynamo parses reasoning before tool calling. For GPT-OSS/Harmony, directed commentary is tool-call text, so Dynamo passes it in normal_text for the Harmony tool parser to emit structured tool_calls, recover final text, and remove tool-call markup from final content.
Harness flags:

vllm: reasoning_parser=openai_gptoss; chat_template_kwargs={}; request.skip_special_tokens=false
sglang: model_type=gpt-oss; stream_reasoning=true; force_reasoning=false

Not set by this parser-level parity harness:
- frontend `tool_choice`

Recipientless Harmony commentary is not applicable to Kimi K2.5

REASONING.batch.3.d — kimi_k25
Directed Harmony commentary tool calls are not applicable to Kimi K2.5
Why n/a:
Kimi K2.5 does not use Harmony `commentary to=functions.*` envelopes; downstream tool calls use Kimi tool-section markers.
n/a
REASONING.batch.3.e — kimi_k25
Directed Harmony analysis tool calls are not applicable to Kimi K2.5
Why n/a:
Kimi K2.5 does not use Harmony `analysis to=functions.*` envelopes; reasoning is represented by think tags.
n/a
REASONING.batch.3.f — kimi_k25
Harmony analysis/commentary/final channel sequencing is not applicable to Kimi K2.5
Why n/a:
Kimi K2.5 has no Harmony channel protocol, so mixed analysis, commentary tool call, and final-channel sequencing is outside its grammar.

REASONING.batch.6.a — kimi_k25
Multiple reasoning spans are concatenated
Input:
input_text="<think>first</think> middle <think>second</think> done"
Dynamo:
reasoning_text="firstsecond"
normal_text="middle  done"
vLLM:
reasoning_text="first"
normal_text=" middle <think>second</think> done"
SGLang:
reasoning_text="first"
normal_text=" middle <think>second</think> done"
Explanations:
vLLM: Dynamo extracts each complete reasoning span; vLLM Kimi K2 parser leaves the later complete span in normal_text.
SGLang: Dynamo extracts every complete reasoning span and concatenates them; SGLang exits reasoning at the first end marker and leaves the later span, with its literal markers, in normal_text.
Harness flags:
Parity harness flags used for this result:
dynamo: parser_family=kimi_k25; in_reasoning=false; token_ids=none
vllm: reasoning_parser=kimi_k2; chat_template_kwargs={}; request.skip_special_tokens=false
sglang: model_type=kimi_k2; stream_reasoning=true; force_reasoning=true

Not set by this parser-level parity harness:
- frontend `tool_choice`
- SGLang `separate_reasoning`
- request `enable_thinking` / `thinking` / `thinking_mode` unless shown in vLLM chat_template_kwargs above
Ref:
inspired by vLLM Kimi K2/K2.5 reasoning tests: https://github.com/vllm-project/vllm/blob/39910f2b25aacc09f5e7f166cdf0030b19f8b9e8/tests/reasoning/test_kimi_k2_reasoning_parser.py; local taxonomy: lib/parsers/REASONING_CASES.md

REASONING.batch.3.b — minimax_append_think
Open reasoning interrupted by downstream tool-call text is not configured for MiniMax append-think
Why n/a:
MiniMax append-think emits a synthetic normal-text wrapper instead of running an open reasoning-span boundary; closed-span handoff is covered by REASONING.batch.3.a.
Ref:

REASONING.batch.2.d — qwen3
Normal text around reasoning
Input:
input_text="before <think>thinking</think> after"
Dynamo:
reasoning_text="thinking"
normal_text="before  after"
vLLM:
reasoning_text="thinking"
normal_text=" after"
SGLang:
reasoning_text="before thinking"
normal_text=" after"
Explanations:
vLLM: Dynamo keeps visible text outside a complete reasoning span as normal_text; vLLM drops the prefix.
SGLang: Dynamo keeps text emitted before the reasoning open marker as normal_text; SGLang strips the start marker in place and folds that prefix into reasoning_text.

REASONING.batch.4 — qwen3
Dangling end marker without an opening think tag
Input:
input_text="normal</think>answer"
Dynamo:
reasoning_text="normal"
normal_text="answer"
vLLM:
reasoning_text="normal"
normal_text="answer"
SGLang:
reasoning_text=""
normal_text="normal</think>answer"
Explanations:
SGLang: Dynamo treats the text before an unpaired end marker as reasoning (implicit-opener recovery, matching vLLM); SGLang enters reasoning only on an explicit start marker, so the dangling end marker and surrounding text stay in normal_text.

REASONING.batch.6.a — qwen3
Multiple reasoning spans are concatenated
Input:
input_text="<think>first</think> middle <think>second</think> done"
Dynamo:
reasoning_text="firstsecond"
normal_text="middle  done"
vLLM:
reasoning_text="first"
normal_text=" middle <think>second</think> done"
SGLang:
reasoning_text="first"
normal_text=" middle <think>second</think> done"
Explanations:
vLLM: Dynamo extracts each complete reasoning span; vLLM leaves the later complete span in normal_text.
SGLang: Dynamo extracts every complete reasoning span and concatenates them; SGLang exits reasoning at the first end marker and leaves the later span, with its literal markers, in normal_text.
Harness flags:
Parity harness flags used for this result:
dynamo: parser_family=qwen3; in_reasoning=false; token_ids=none
vllm: reasoning_parser=qwen3; chat_template_kwargs={}; request.skip_special_tokens=false
sglang: model_type=qwen3; stream_reasoning=true; force_reasoning=false

Not set by this parser-level parity harness:
- frontend `tool_choice`
- SGLang `separate_reasoning`
- request `enable_thinking` / `thinking` / `thinking_mode` unless shown in vLLM chat_template_kwargs above
Ref:
inspired by vLLM Qwen3 reasoning tests: https://github.com/vllm-project/vllm/blob/39910f2b25aacc09f5e7f166cdf0030b19f8b9e8/tests/reasoning/test_qwen3_reasoning_parser.py; local taxonomy: lib/parsers/REASONING_CASES.md
Spec ref:
lib/parsers/REASONING_CASES.md; https://qwen.readthedocs.io/en/stable/inference/transformers.html#parsing-thinking-content; https://docs.nvidia.com/dynamo/dev/user-guides/reasoning/reasoning-parsing-dynamo

REASONING.batch.3.b — deepseek_v3
Open reasoning interrupted by downstream tool-call text is not configured for DeepSeek V3
Why n/a:
Dynamo's DeepSeek V3 reasoning parser has no downstream tool-call boundary while reasoning is open; closed-span handoff is covered by REASONING.batch.3.a.
Ref:
inspired by vLLM DeepSeek V3 reasoning tests: https://github.com/vllm-project/vllm/blob/39910f2b25aacc09f5e7f166cdf0030b19f8b9e8/tests/reasoning/test_deepseekv3_reasoning_parser.py; local taxonomy: lib/parsers/REASONING_CASES.md
n/a
REASONING.batch.3.c — deepseek_v3
Recipientless Harmony commentary is not applicable to DeepSeek V3
Why n/a:
DeepSeek V3 does not use Harmony commentary channels; visible text and downstream tool handoff use DeepSeek-specific think and tool-call markers.
n/a
REASONING.batch.3.d — deepseek_v3
Directed Harmony commentary tool calls are not applicable to DeepSeek V3
Why n/a:
DeepSeek V3 does not use Harmony `commentary to=functions.*` envelopes; downstream tool calls use DeepSeek-specific tool-call markers.
n/a
REASONING.batch.3.e — deepseek_v3
Directed Harmony analysis tool calls are not applicable to DeepSeek V3
Why n/a:
DeepSeek V3 does not use Harmony `analysis to=functions.*` envelopes; reasoning is represented by think tags.
n/a
REASONING.batch.3.f — deepseek_v3
Harmony analysis/commentary/final channel sequencing is not applicable to DeepSeek V3
Why n/a:
DeepSeek V3 has no Harmony channel protocol, so mixed analysis, commentary tool call, and final-channel sequencing is outside its grammar.

REASONING.batch.4 — deepseek_v3
Thinking-mode completion exits on a dangling end marker
Input:
input_text="normal</think>answer"
Dynamo:
reasoning_text="normal"
normal_text="answer"
vLLM:
reasoning_text="normal"
normal_text="answer"
SGLang:
reasoning_text=""
normal_text="normal</think>answer"
Explanations:
SGLang: Dynamo/vLLM treat a dangling end marker as the close for force-reasoning content; SGLang only enters reasoning after an explicit start marker.

REASONING.batch.6.a — deepseek_v3
Multiple reasoning spans are concatenated by Dynamo
Input:
input_text="<think>first</think> middle <think>second</think> done"
Dynamo:
reasoning_text="firstsecond"
normal_text="middle  done"
vLLM:
reasoning_text="first"
normal_text=" middle <think>second</think> done"
SGLang:
reasoning_text="first"
normal_text=" middle <think>second</think> done"
Explanations:
vLLM: Dynamo extracts each complete reasoning span; vLLM leaves the later complete span in normal_text.
SGLang: Dynamo extracts every complete reasoning span and concatenates them; SGLang exits reasoning at the first end marker and leaves the later span in normal_text.
Harness flags:
Parity harness flags used for this result:
dynamo: parser_family=deepseek_v3; in_reasoning=false; token_ids=none
vllm: reasoning_parser=deepseek_v3; chat_template_kwargs={"thinking": true}; request.skip_special_tokens=false
sglang: model_type=deepseek-v3; stream_reasoning=true; force_reasoning=false

Not set by this parser-level parity harness:
- frontend `tool_choice`
- SGLang `separate_reasoning`
- request `enable_thinking` / `thinking` / `thinking_mode` unless shown in vLLM chat_template_kwargs above
Ref:
inspired by vLLM DeepSeek V3 reasoning tests: https://github.com/vllm-project/vllm/blob/39910f2b25aacc09f5e7f166cdf0030b19f8b9e8/tests/reasoning/test_deepseekv3_reasoning_parser.py; local taxonomy: lib/parsers/REASONING_CASES.md
Spec ref:
lib/parsers/REASONING_CASES.md; https://api-docs.deepseek.com/guides/thinking_mode; https://docs.nvidia.com/dynamo/dev/user-guides/reasoning/reasoning-parsing-dynamo

REASONING.batch.6.a — deepseek_v3
Multiple reasoning spans are concatenated by Dynamo
Input:
input_text="<think>first</think> middle <think>second</think> done"
Dynamo:
reasoning_text="firstsecond"
normal_text="middle  done"
vLLM:
reasoning_text="first"
normal_text=" middle <think>second</think> done"
SGLang:
reasoning_text="first"
normal_text=" middle <think>second</think> done"
Explanations:
vLLM: Dynamo extracts each complete reasoning span; vLLM leaves the later complete span in normal_text.
SGLang: Dynamo extracts every complete reasoning span and concatenates them; SGLang exits reasoning at the first end marker and leaves the later span in normal_text.
Harness flags:
Parity harness flags used for this result:
dynamo: parser_family=deepseek_v3; in_reasoning=false; token_ids=none
vllm: reasoning_parser=deepseek_v3; chat_template_kwargs={"thinking": true}; request.skip_special_tokens=false
sglang: model_type=deepseek-v3; stream_reasoning=true; force_reasoning=false

Not set by this parser-level parity harness:
- frontend `tool_choice`
- SGLang `separate_reasoning`
- request `enable_thinking` / `thinking` / `thinking_mode` unless shown in vLLM chat_template_kwargs above

lib/parsers/REASONING_CASES.md; https://api-docs.deepseek.com/guides/thinking_mode; https://docs.nvidia.com/dynamo/dev/user-guides/reasoning/reasoning-parsing-dynamo

REASONING.batch.3.e — deepseek_v3

n/a
REASONING.batch.3.f — deepseek_v3
Harmony analysis/commentary/final channel sequencing is not applicable to DeepSeek V3
Why n/a:
DeepSeek V3 has no Harmony channel protocol, so mixed analysis, commentary tool call, and final-channel sequencing is outside its grammar.

normal_text="[TOOL_CALLS][{"name": "get_weather", "arguments": {"location": "NYC"}}][/TOOL_CALLS]"

REASONING.batch.3.b — mistral
Open reasoning interrupted by downstream tool-call text is not configured for Mistral
Why n/a:
Dynamo's Mistral reasoning parser has no downstream tool-call boundary while reasoning is open; closed-span handoff is covered by REASONING.batch.3.a.
Ref:
inspired by vLLM Mistral reasoning tests: https://github.com/vllm-project/vllm/blob/39910f2b25aacc09f5e7f166cdf0030b19f8b9e8/tests/reasoning/test_mistral_reasoning_parser.py; local taxonomy: lib/parsers/REASONING_CASES.md
n/a
REASONING.batch.3.c — mistral
Recipientless Harmony commentary is not applicable to Mistral
Why n/a:
Mistral reasoning parsers do not use Harmony commentary channels; visible text and downstream tool handoff use Mistral-specific reasoning and tool-call markers.
n/a
REASONING.batch.3.d — mistral
Directed Harmony commentary tool calls are not applicable to Mistral
Why n/a:
Mistral reasoning parsers do not use Harmony `commentary to=functions.*` envelopes; downstream tool calls use Mistral-specific tool-call markers.
n/a
REASONING.batch.3.e — mistral
Directed Harmony analysis tool calls are not applicable to Mistral
Why n/a:
Mistral reasoning parsers do not use Harmony `analysis to=functions.*` envelopes; reasoning is represented by Mistral THINK tags.
n/a
REASONING.batch.3.f — mistral
Harmony analysis/commentary/final channel sequencing is not applicable to Mistral
Why n/a:
Mistral reasoning parsers have no Harmony channel protocol, so mixed analysis, commentary tool call, and final-channel sequencing is outside their grammar.

REASONING.batch.2.d — nemotron_deci
Normal text around reasoning
Input:
input_text="before <think>thinking</think> after"
Dynamo:
reasoning_text="thinking"
normal_text="before  after"
vLLM:
reasoning_text="thinking"
normal_text=" after"
SGLang:
reasoning_text="before thinking"
normal_text=" after"
Explanations:
vLLM: Dynamo keeps visible text outside a complete reasoning span as normal_text; vLLM drops the prefix.
SGLang: Dynamo keeps text emitted before the reasoning open marker as normal_text; SGLang strips the start marker in place and folds that prefix into reasoning_text.

REASONING.batch.4 — nemotron_deci
Dangling end marker without an opening think tag

REASONING.batch.6.a — nemotron_deci
Multiple reasoning spans are concatenated by Dynamo
Input:
input_text="<think>first</think> middle <think>second</think> done"
Dynamo:
reasoning_text="firstsecond"
normal_text="middle  done"
vLLM:
reasoning_text="first"
normal_text=" middle <think>second</think> done"
SGLang:
reasoning_text="first"
normal_text=" middle <think>second</think> done"
Explanations:
vLLM: Dynamo extracts each complete reasoning span; vLLM leaves the later complete span in normal_text.
SGLang: Dynamo extracts every complete reasoning span and concatenates them; SGLang exits reasoning at the first end marker and leaves the later span, with its literal markers, in normal_text.
Harness flags:
Parity harness flags used for this result:
dynamo: parser_family=nemotron_deci; in_reasoning=false; token_ids=none
vllm: reasoning_parser=glm45; chat_template_kwargs={}; request.skip_special_tokens=false
sglang: model_type=glm45; stream_reasoning=true; force_reasoning=false

Not set by this parser-level parity harness:
- frontend `tool_choice`
- SGLang `separate_reasoning`
- request `enable_thinking` / `thinking` / `thinking_mode` unless shown in vLLM chat_template_kwargs above
Ref:

REASONING.batch.3.b — deepseek_r1
Open reasoning interrupted by downstream tool-call text is not configured for DeepSeek R1-family parsing
Why n/a:
Dynamo's DeepSeek R1-family reasoning parser has no downstream tool-call boundary while reasoning is open; closed-span handoff is covered by REASONING.batch.3.a.
Ref:
inspired by vLLM DeepSeek R1 reasoning tests: https://github.com/vllm-project/vllm/blob/39910f2b25aacc09f5e7f166cdf0030b19f8b9e8/tests/reasoning/test_deepseekr1_reasoning_parser.py; local taxonomy: lib/parsers/REASONING_CASES.md
n/a
REASONING.batch.3.c — deepseek_r1
Recipientless Harmony commentary is not applicable to DeepSeek R1-family parsers
Why n/a:
DeepSeek R1-family parsers do not use Harmony commentary channels; visible text and downstream tool handoff use model-specific think and tool-call markers.
n/a
REASONING.batch.3.d — deepseek_r1
Directed Harmony commentary tool calls are not applicable to DeepSeek R1-family parsers
Why n/a:
DeepSeek R1-family parsers do not use Harmony `commentary to=functions.*` envelopes; downstream tool calls use model-specific tool-call markers.
n/a
REASONING.batch.3.e — deepseek_r1
Directed Harmony analysis tool calls are not applicable to DeepSeek R1-family parsers
Why n/a:
DeepSeek R1-family parsers do not use Harmony `analysis to=functions.*` envelopes; reasoning is represented by think tags.
n/a
REASONING.batch.3.f — deepseek_r1
Harmony analysis/commentary/final channel sequencing is not applicable to DeepSeek R1-family parsers
Why n/a:
DeepSeek R1-family parsers have no Harmony channel protocol, so mixed analysis, commentary tool call, and final-channel sequencing is outside their grammar.

REASONING.batch.6.a — deepseek_r1
Multiple reasoning spans are concatenated by Dynamo
Input:
input_text="<think>first</think> middle <think>second</think> done"
Dynamo:
reasoning_text="firstsecond"
normal_text="middle  done"
vLLM:
reasoning_text="first"
normal_text=" middle <think>second</think> done"
SGLang:
reasoning_text="first"
normal_text=" middle <think>second</think> done"
Explanations:
vLLM: Dynamo extracts each complete reasoning span; vLLM leaves the later complete span in normal_text.
SGLang: Dynamo extracts every complete reasoning span and concatenates them; SGLang exits reasoning at the first end marker and leaves the later span in normal_text.
Harness flags:
Parity harness flags used for this result:
dynamo: parser_family=deepseek_r1; in_reasoning=false; token_ids=none
vllm: reasoning_parser=deepseek_r1; chat_template_kwargs={}; request.skip_special_tokens=false
sglang: model_type=deepseek-r1; stream_reasoning=true; force_reasoning=false

Not set by this parser-level parity harness:
- frontend `tool_choice`
- SGLang `separate_reasoning`
- request `enable_thinking` / `thinking` / `thinking_mode` unless shown in vLLM chat_template_kwargs above
Ref:
inspired by vLLM DeepSeek R1 reasoning tests: https://github.com/vllm-project/vllm/blob/39910f2b25aacc09f5e7f166cdf0030b19f8b9e8/tests/reasoning/test_deepseekr1_reasoning_parser.py; local taxonomy: lib/parsers/REASONING_CASES.md
Spec ref:
lib/parsers/REASONING_CASES.md; https://docs.nvidia.com/dynamo/dev/user-guides/reasoning/reasoning-parsing-dynamo

Legend: = all captured peers match Dynamo · D Dynamo-only fixture (both peers unavailable) · V/S divergence (V = vLLM, S = SGLang; intentional, has reason:) · ? more research needed (e.g. V?, S? — diverges with no reason: yet) · ↯ Dynamo leaks reasoning markup or final-answer text · ! expected-error suffix (e.g. V!, S! — engine crashes by design) · n/a not applicable.
† = no vLLM peer reasoning parser for this family · § = no SGLang peer reasoning parser for this family.

Tooltip fields: input_text=raw model output or stream chunks fed into the reasoning parser · reasoning_text=hidden reasoning content extracted by the parser · normal_text=residual text passed onward to response assembly or downstream parsers · harness flags=the exact parser-level arguments used for the parity result.

Omitted tool calling parser rows: no corresponding Dynamo reasoning parser fixture for AI21 Jamba (jamba), Hermes-3 / Llama variants (hermes), Llama 3 (JSON fmt) (llama3_json), Llama 4 (pythonic fmt) (pythonic), Phi-4 (phi4), Qwen 2.5 (qwen25).

Stats: 15 families × 16 sub-cases = 240 grid slots (78 n/a, 0 missing). 162 real cases: 111 captured-peer parity · 0 Dynamo-only · 37 documented divergences (have reason:) · 14 research-needed (no reason: yet) · 0 expected-errors.

Case descriptions

Full case definitions: lib/parsers/REASONING_CASES.md.

Core
REASONING.batch.1.aEmpty input — empty model text. Parser must not crash and must produce coherent empty output
REASONING.batch.1.bPlain text, no reasoning markers — non-empty model text with no reasoning wrapper. Parser must not invent `reasoning_text`
Reasoning extraction
REASONING.batch.2.aReasoning-only span — `<think>...</think>` (or analog) present, with no visible answer text outside the span
REASONING.batch.2.cReasoning followed by visible answer text — reasoning content goes to `reasoning_text`; final answer text goes to `normal_text`
REASONING.batch.2.dVisible text around reasoning — user-visible text appears on both sides of the reasoning span
REASONING.batch.2.eEmpty reasoning span — `<think></think>` (or analog with zero bytes between markers). Must still register as a reasoning span if the family exposes empty spans
REASONING.batch.2.fComplex reasoning body — large blocks, multi-paragraph, special characters, Unicode, newlines, and marker-looking strings inside the reasoning body
Tool call boundary
REASONING.batch.3.aClosed reasoning followed by downstream tool-call text — reasoning parser must extract the think content **and leave a valid paired-parser tool-call payload intact in `normal_text`** for the downstream tool-call parser to consume
REASONING.batch.3.bOpen reasoning interrupted by downstream tool-call text — tool-call markers can terminate or escape an open reasoning span for families that define that boundary
REASONING.batch.3.cRecipientless downstream channel text — format-specific non-tool commentary or equivalent content should remain visible as normal text
REASONING.batch.3.dDirected downstream tool-call channel without reasoning — parser must suppress tool-call payload from visible normal text when that payload belongs to the downstream tool parser
REASONING.batch.3.eDirected reasoning-channel tool-call payload — parser must keep the payload in reasoning output when the format labels the channel as reasoning/analysis
REASONING.batch.3.fReasoning, downstream directed tool call, then final answer — parser must extract reasoning, suppress downstream tool payload from visible normal text, and preserve later final text
Malformed / recovery
REASONING.batch.4Malformed reasoning marker syntax — dangling close marker, invalid channel marker, or marker that does not belong to the family grammar
REASONING.batch.5Missing end-marker recovery — engine hit `max_tokens` mid-think; pin behavior: recover partial reasoning, surface as truncated, or treat all as `normal_text`
Multi-span
REASONING.batch.6.aMultiple reasoning spans, adjacent or separated by normal text — e.g., two `<think>...</think>` blocks in one response. Behavior is impl-defined: concatenate, surface only the first, or document a divergence
1.a1.b2.a2.b3.a3.b3.c4.a4.b4.c
Top-N models

REASONING.stream.2.b — deepseek_v4
Multiple reasoning spans across chunks
Input chunks:
chunks=[
  0: "<think>first</think>"
  1: " middle "
  2: "<think>second</think> done"
]
Dynamo:
reasoning_text="firstsecond"
normal_text=" middle  done"
vLLM:
reasoning_text="first"
normal_text=" middle <think>second</think> done"
SGLang:
reasoning_text="first"
normal_text=" middle <think>second</think> done"
Explanations:
vLLM: Dynamo extracts each complete reasoning span across chunks; vLLM leaves the later complete span in normal_text.
SGLang: Dynamo re-enters reasoning on each open marker across chunks and concatenates all spans; SGLang exits at the first end marker and does not re-enter, leaving the later span in normal_text.
Harness flags:
Parity harness flags used for this result:
dynamo: parser_family=deepseek_v4; in_reasoning=false; token_chunks=none
vllm: reasoning_parser=deepseek_v4; chat_template_kwargs={"enable_thinking": true}; delta_token_ids=derived from stub tokenizer
sglang: model_type=deepseek-v4; stream_reasoning=true; force_reasoning=false

Not set by this parser-level parity harness:
- frontend `tool_choice`
- SGLang `separate_reasoning`
- request `enable_thinking` / `thinking` / `thinking_mode` unless shown in vLLM chat_template_kwargs above
Ref:
inspired by vLLM DeepSeek V4 alias coverage in DeepSeek V3 reasoning tests: https://github.com/vllm-project/vllm/blob/39910f2b25aacc09f5e7f166cdf0030b19f8b9e8/tests/reasoning/test_deepseekv3_reasoning_parser.py; local taxonomy: lib/parsers/REASONING_CASES.md
Spec ref:
lib/parsers/REASONING_CASES.md; https://api-docs.deepseek.com/guides/thinking_mode; https://docs.nvidia.com/dynamo/dev/user-guides/reasoning/reasoning-parsing-dynamo

REASONING.stream.3.b — deepseek_v4
End marker split across chunks
Input chunks:
chunks=[
  0: "<think>thinking</th"
  1: "ink>answer"
]
Dynamo:
reasoning_text="thinking"
normal_text="answer"
vLLM:
reasoning_text="<think>thinking</think>answer"
normal_text=""
SGLang:
reasoning_text="thinking</think>answer"
normal_text=""
Explanations:
vLLM: Dynamo buffers a split end delimiter and resumes normal_text after it; vLLM keeps the delimiter and answer in reasoning_text.
SGLang: Dynamo buffers an end marker split across chunk boundaries and resumes normal_text after it; SGLang streams the partial delimiter as reasoning (it only holds back a partial marker when the whole pending buffer is a marker prefix), so the split marker is never reassembled and the answer stays in reasoning_text.
Harness flags:
Parity harness flags used for this result:
dynamo: parser_family=deepseek_v4; in_reasoning=false; token_chunks=none
vllm: reasoning_parser=deepseek_v4; chat_template_kwargs={"enable_thinking": true}; delta_token_ids=derived from stub tokenizer
sglang: model_type=deepseek-v4; stream_reasoning=true; force_reasoning=false

Not set by this parser-level parity harness:
- frontend `tool_choice`
- SGLang `separate_reasoning`
- request `enable_thinking` / `thinking` / `thinking_mode` unless shown in vLLM chat_template_kwargs above

Why n/a:
DeepSeek V4 has no Harmony commentary protocol, so partial commentary-boundary recovery is outside its grammar.

REASONING.stream.2.b — glm45
Multiple reasoning spans across chunks
Input chunks:
chunks=[
  0: "<think>first</think>"
  1: " middle "
  2: "<think>second</think> done"
]
Dynamo:
reasoning_text="firstsecond"
normal_text=" middle  done"
vLLM:
reasoning_text="first"
normal_text=" middle <think>second</think> done"
SGLang:
reasoning_text="first"
normal_text=" middle <think>second</think> done"
Family mapping:
This row uses the public GLM/Nemotron reasoning parser family 'glm45'; fixtures are shared with 'nemotron_deci' because GLM and Nemotron use the same parser implementation here.
Explanations:
vLLM: Dynamo extracts each complete reasoning span across chunks; vLLM leaves the later complete span in normal_text.
SGLang: Dynamo re-enters reasoning on each open marker across chunks and concatenates all spans; SGLang exits at the first end marker and does not re-enter, leaving the later span in normal_text.
Harness flags:
Parity harness flags used for this result:
dynamo: parser_family=glm45; fixture_family=nemotron_deci; in_reasoning=false; token_chunks=none
vllm: reasoning_parser=glm45; chat_template_kwargs={}; delta_token_ids=derived from stub tokenizer
sglang: model_type=glm45; stream_reasoning=true; force_reasoning=false

Not set by this parser-level parity harness:
- frontend `tool_choice`
- SGLang `separate_reasoning`
- request `enable_thinking` / `thinking` / `thinking_mode` unless shown in vLLM chat_template_kwargs above
Ref:
inspired by vLLM GLM/Nemotron think-tag reasoning tests: https://github.com/vllm-project/vllm/blob/39910f2b25aacc09f5e7f166cdf0030b19f8b9e8/tests/reasoning/test_glm4_moe_reasoning_parser.py and https://github.com/vllm-project/vllm/blob/39910f2b25aacc09f5e7f166cdf0030b19f8b9e8/tests/reasoning/test_nemotron_v3_reasoning_parser.py; local taxonomy: lib/parsers/REASONING_CASES.md

REASONING.stream.3.b — glm45
End marker split across chunks
Input chunks:
chunks=[
  0: "<think>thinking</th"
  1: "ink>answer"
]
Dynamo:
reasoning_text="thinking"
normal_text="answer"
vLLM:
reasoning_text="<think>thinking</think>answer"
normal_text=""
SGLang:
reasoning_text="thinking</think>answer"
normal_text=""
Family mapping:
This row uses the public GLM/Nemotron reasoning parser family 'glm45'; fixtures are shared with 'nemotron_deci' because GLM and Nemotron use the same parser implementation here.
Explanations:
vLLM: Dynamo buffers a split end delimiter and resumes normal_text after it; vLLM keeps the delimiter and answer in reasoning_text.
SGLang: Dynamo buffers an end marker split across chunk boundaries and resumes normal_text after it; SGLang streams the partial delimiter as reasoning (it only holds back a partial marker when the whole pending buffer is a marker prefix), so the split marker is never reassembled and the answer stays in reasoning_text.
Harness flags:
Parity harness flags used for this result:
dynamo: parser_family=glm45; fixture_family=nemotron_deci; in_reasoning=false; token_chunks=none
vllm: reasoning_parser=glm45; chat_template_kwargs={}; delta_token_ids=derived from stub tokenizer
sglang: model_type=glm45; stream_reasoning=true; force_reasoning=false

Not set by this parser-level parity harness:
- frontend `tool_choice`
- SGLang `separate_reasoning`
- request `enable_thinking` / `thinking` / `thinking_mode` unless shown in vLLM chat_template_kwargs above

inspired by vLLM GLM/Nemotron think-tag reasoning tests: https://github.com/vllm-project/vllm/blob/39910f2b25aacc09f5e7f166cdf0030b19f8b9e8/tests/reasoning/test_glm4_moe_reasoning_parser.py and https://github.com/vllm-project/vllm/blob/39910f2b25aacc09f5e7f166cdf0030b19f8b9e8/tests/reasoning/test_nemotron_v3_reasoning_parser.py; local taxonomy: lib/parsers/REASONING_CASES.md

REASONING.stream.4.b — gpt_oss
Directed Harmony commentary tool recipient split across chunks
Input chunks:
chunks=[
  0: "<|channel|>commentary to=functions.get_"
  1: "weather <|constrain|>json<|message|>{"city":"SF"}<|call|>"
]
Dynamo:
reasoning_text=""
normal_text="<|channel|>commentary to=functions.get_weather <|constrain|>json<|message|>{"city":"SF"}<|call|>"
vLLM:
reasoning_text=""
normal_text=""
SGLang:
reasoning_text=""
normal_text="<|channel|>commentary to=functions.get_weather <|constrain|>json<|message|>{"city":"SF"}<|call|>"
Explanations:
vLLM: vLLM streaming reasoning suppresses directed Harmony commentary at the reasoning layer; Dynamo keeps it because normal_text is the handoff to the Harmony tool parser.
Dynamo: Unlike vLLM streaming reasoning, Dynamo parses reasoning before tool calling. For GPT-OSS/Harmony, directed commentary is tool-call text, so Dynamo passes it in normal_text for the Harmony tool parser to emit structured tool_calls and remove the markup from final content.
Harness flags:
Parity harness flags used for this result:
dynamo: parser_family=gpt_oss; in_reasoning=false; token_chunks=none
vllm: reasoning_parser=openai_gptoss; chat_template_kwargs={}; delta_token_ids=derived from Harmony tokenizer
sglang: model_type=gpt-oss; stream_reasoning=true; force_reasoning=false

Not set by this parser-level parity harness:
- frontend `tool_choice`
- SGLang `separate_reasoning`
- request `enable_thinking` / `thinking` / `thinking_mode` unless shown in vLLM chat_template_kwargs above
Ref:
inspired by vLLM GPT-OSS reasoning tests: https://github.com/vllm-project/vllm/blob/39910f2b25aacc09f5e7f166cdf0030b19f8b9e8/tests/reasoning/test_gptoss_reasoning_parser.py; local taxonomy: lib/parsers/REASONING_CASES.md

REASONING.stream.2.b — kimi_k25
Multiple reasoning spans across chunks
Input chunks:
chunks=[
  0: "<think>first</think>"
  1: " middle "
  2: "<think>second</think> done"
]
Dynamo:
reasoning_text="firstsecond"
normal_text=" middle  done"
vLLM:
reasoning_text="<think>first"
normal_text=" middle <think>second</think> done"
SGLang:
reasoning_text="first"
normal_text=" middle <think>second</think> done"
Explanations:
vLLM: vLLM Kimi K2 streaming parser leaks the first start marker and leaves the later complete span in normal_text.
SGLang: Dynamo re-enters reasoning on each open marker across chunks and concatenates all spans; SGLang exits at the first end marker and does not re-enter, leaving the later span in normal_text.
Harness flags:
Parity harness flags used for this result:
dynamo: parser_family=kimi_k25; in_reasoning=false; token_chunks=none
vllm: reasoning_parser=kimi_k2; chat_template_kwargs={}; delta_token_ids=derived from stub tokenizer
sglang: model_type=kimi_k2; stream_reasoning=true; force_reasoning=true

Not set by this parser-level parity harness:
- frontend `tool_choice`
- SGLang `separate_reasoning`
- request `enable_thinking` / `thinking` / `thinking_mode` unless shown in vLLM chat_template_kwargs above
Ref:
inspired by vLLM Kimi K2/K2.5 reasoning tests: https://github.com/vllm-project/vllm/blob/39910f2b25aacc09f5e7f166cdf0030b19f8b9e8/tests/reasoning/test_kimi_k2_reasoning_parser.py; local taxonomy: lib/parsers/REASONING_CASES.md

REASONING.stream.3.b — kimi_k25
End marker split across chunks
Input chunks:
chunks=[
  0: "<think>thinking</th"
  1: "ink>answer"
]
Dynamo:
reasoning_text="thinking"
normal_text="answer"
vLLM:
reasoning_text="<think>thinking</think>answer"
normal_text=""
SGLang:
reasoning_text="thinking</think>answer"
normal_text=""
Explanations:
vLLM: Dynamo buffers a split end delimiter and resumes normal_text after it; vLLM Kimi K2 streaming parser keeps the delimiter and answer in reasoning_text.
SGLang: Dynamo buffers an end marker split across chunk boundaries and resumes normal_text after it; SGLang streams the partial delimiter as reasoning (it only holds back a partial marker when the whole pending buffer is a marker prefix), so the split marker is never reassembled and the answer stays in reasoning_text.
Harness flags:
Parity harness flags used for this result:
dynamo: parser_family=kimi_k25; in_reasoning=false; token_chunks=none

- frontend `tool_choice`
- SGLang `separate_reasoning`
- request `enable_thinking` / `thinking` / `thinking_mode` unless shown in vLLM chat_template_kwargs above

REASONING.stream.3.b — qwen3
End marker split across chunks
Input chunks:
chunks=[
  0: "<think>thinking</th"
  1: "ink>answer"
]
Dynamo:
reasoning_text="thinking"
normal_text="answer"
vLLM:
reasoning_text="thinking</think>answer"
normal_text=""
SGLang:
reasoning_text="thinking</think>answer"
normal_text=""
Explanations:
vLLM: Dynamo buffers a split end delimiter and resumes normal_text after it; vLLM keeps the delimiter and answer in reasoning_text.
SGLang: Dynamo buffers an end marker split across chunk boundaries and resumes normal_text after it; SGLang streams the partial delimiter as reasoning (it only holds back a partial marker when the whole pending buffer is a marker prefix), so the split marker is never reassembled and the answer stays in reasoning_text.
Harness flags:
Parity harness flags used for this result:
dynamo: parser_family=qwen3; in_reasoning=false; token_chunks=none

REASONING.stream.4.a — qwen3
Downstream streaming boundary is not applicable to Qwen3
Why n/a:

REASONING.stream.4.b — qwen3
Split downstream streaming boundary is not applicable to Qwen3
Why n/a:
Qwen3 has no configured tool-call start marker that force-exits open streaming reasoning, so there is no split downstream boundary to buffer.
n/a
REASONING.stream.4.c — qwen3
Partial downstream boundary recovery is not applicable to Qwen3
Why n/a:
Qwen3 has no configured tool-call start marker that force-exits open streaming reasoning, so partial tool-marker recovery is outside its grammar.

REASONING.stream.2.b — deepseek_v3
Multiple reasoning spans across chunks
Input chunks:
chunks=[
  0: "<think>first</think>"
  1: " middle "
  2: "<think>second</think> done"
]
Dynamo:
reasoning_text="firstsecond"
normal_text=" middle  done"
vLLM:
reasoning_text="first"
normal_text=" middle <think>second</think> done"
SGLang:
reasoning_text="first"
normal_text=" middle <think>second</think> done"
Explanations:
vLLM: Dynamo extracts each complete reasoning span across chunks; vLLM leaves the later complete span in normal_text.
SGLang: Dynamo re-enters reasoning on each open marker across chunks and concatenates all spans; SGLang exits at the first end marker and does not re-enter, leaving the later span in normal_text.
Harness flags:
Parity harness flags used for this result:
dynamo: parser_family=deepseek_v3; in_reasoning=false; token_chunks=none
vllm: reasoning_parser=deepseek_v3; chat_template_kwargs={"thinking": true}; delta_token_ids=derived from stub tokenizer
sglang: model_type=deepseek-v3; stream_reasoning=true; force_reasoning=false

Not set by this parser-level parity harness:
- frontend `tool_choice`
- SGLang `separate_reasoning`
- request `enable_thinking` / `thinking` / `thinking_mode` unless shown in vLLM chat_template_kwargs above

REASONING.stream.2.b — deepseek_v3
Multiple reasoning spans across chunks
Input chunks:
chunks=[
  0: "<think>first</think>"
  1: " middle "
  2: "<think>second</think> done"
]
Dynamo:
reasoning_text="firstsecond"
normal_text=" middle  done"
vLLM:
reasoning_text="first"
normal_text=" middle <think>second</think> done"
SGLang:
reasoning_text="first"
normal_text=" middle <think>second</think> done"
Explanations:
vLLM: Dynamo extracts each complete reasoning span across chunks; vLLM leaves the later complete span in normal_text.
SGLang: Dynamo re-enters reasoning on each open marker across chunks and concatenates all spans; SGLang exits at the first end marker and does not re-enter, leaving the later span in normal_text.
Harness flags:
Parity harness flags used for this result:
dynamo: parser_family=deepseek_v3; in_reasoning=false; token_chunks=none
vllm: reasoning_parser=deepseek_v3; chat_template_kwargs={"thinking": true}; delta_token_ids=derived from stub tokenizer
sglang: model_type=deepseek-v3; stream_reasoning=true; force_reasoning=false

Not set by this parser-level parity harness:
- frontend `tool_choice`
- SGLang `separate_reasoning`
- request `enable_thinking` / `thinking` / `thinking_mode` unless shown in vLLM chat_template_kwargs above

inspired by vLLM DeepSeek V3 reasoning tests: https://github.com/vllm-project/vllm/blob/39910f2b25aacc09f5e7f166cdf0030b19f8b9e8/tests/reasoning/test_deepseekv3_reasoning_parser.py; local taxonomy: lib/parsers/REASONING_CASES.md

REASONING.stream.4.c — mistral

Why n/a:
Mistral has no Harmony commentary protocol, so partial commentary-boundary recovery is outside its grammar.

REASONING.stream.2.a — nemotron_deci
Single reasoning block across chunks

  1: "king</think>"
  2: "answer"

normal_text="answer"
SGLang:
reasoning_text="thinking"
normal_text="answer"

REASONING.stream.2.b — nemotron_deci
Multiple reasoning spans across chunks
Input chunks:
chunks=[
  0: "<think>first</think>"
  1: " middle "
  2: "<think>second</think> done"
]
Dynamo:
reasoning_text="firstsecond"
normal_text=" middle  done"
vLLM:
reasoning_text="first"
normal_text=" middle <think>second</think> done"
SGLang:
reasoning_text="first"
normal_text=" middle <think>second</think> done"
Explanations:
vLLM: Dynamo extracts each complete reasoning span across chunks; vLLM leaves the later complete span in normal_text.
SGLang: Dynamo re-enters reasoning on each open marker across chunks and concatenates all spans; SGLang exits at the first end marker and does not re-enter, leaving the later span in normal_text.
Harness flags:
Parity harness flags used for this result:
dynamo: parser_family=nemotron_deci; in_reasoning=false; token_chunks=none
vllm: reasoning_parser=glm45; chat_template_kwargs={}; delta_token_ids=derived from stub tokenizer
sglang: model_type=glm45; stream_reasoning=true; force_reasoning=false

Not set by this parser-level parity harness:
- frontend `tool_choice`
- SGLang `separate_reasoning`
- request `enable_thinking` / `thinking` / `thinking_mode` unless shown in vLLM chat_template_kwargs above
Ref:
inspired by vLLM GLM/Nemotron think-tag reasoning tests: https://github.com/vllm-project/vllm/blob/39910f2b25aacc09f5e7f166cdf0030b19f8b9e8/tests/reasoning/test_glm4_moe_reasoning_parser.py and https://github.com/vllm-project/vllm/blob/39910f2b25aacc09f5e7f166cdf0030b19f8b9e8/tests/reasoning/test_nemotron_v3_reasoning_parser.py; local taxonomy: lib/parsers/REASONING_CASES.md

REASONING.stream.3.b — nemotron_deci
End marker split across chunks
Input chunks:
chunks=[
  0: "<think>thinking</th"
  1: "ink>answer"
]
Dynamo:
reasoning_text="thinking"
normal_text="answer"
vLLM:
reasoning_text="<think>thinking</think>answer"
normal_text=""
SGLang:
reasoning_text="thinking</think>answer"
normal_text=""
Explanations:
vLLM: Dynamo buffers a split end delimiter and resumes normal_text after it; vLLM keeps the delimiter and answer in reasoning_text.
SGLang: Dynamo buffers an end marker split across chunk boundaries and resumes normal_text after it; SGLang streams the partial delimiter as reasoning (it only holds back a partial marker when the whole pending buffer is a marker prefix), so the split marker is never reassembled and the answer stays in reasoning_text.
Harness flags:
Parity harness flags used for this result:
dynamo: parser_family=nemotron_deci; in_reasoning=false; token_chunks=none
vllm: reasoning_parser=glm45; chat_template_kwargs={}; delta_token_ids=derived from stub tokenizer
sglang: model_type=glm45; stream_reasoning=true; force_reasoning=false

Not set by this parser-level parity harness:
- frontend `tool_choice`
- SGLang `separate_reasoning`
- request `enable_thinking` / `thinking` / `thinking_mode` unless shown in vLLM chat_template_kwargs above

inspired by vLLM GLM/Nemotron think-tag reasoning tests: https://github.com/vllm-project/vllm/blob/39910f2b25aacc09f5e7f166cdf0030b19f8b9e8/tests/reasoning/test_glm4_moe_reasoning_parser.py and https://github.com/vllm-project/vllm/blob/39910f2b25aacc09f5e7f166cdf0030b19f8b9e8/tests/reasoning/test_nemotron_v3_reasoning_parser.py; local taxonomy: lib/parsers/REASONING_CASES.md

REASONING.stream.3.b — deepseek_r1
End marker split across chunks
Input chunks:
chunks=[
  0: "<think>thinking</th"
  1: "ink>answer"
]
Dynamo:
reasoning_text="thinking"
normal_text="answer"
vLLM:
reasoning_text="<think>thinking</think>answer"
normal_text=""
SGLang:
reasoning_text="thinking</think>answer"
normal_text=""
Explanations:
vLLM: Dynamo buffers a split end delimiter and resumes normal_text after it; vLLM keeps the delimiter and answer in reasoning_text.
SGLang: Dynamo buffers an end marker split across chunk boundaries and resumes normal_text after it; SGLang streams the partial delimiter as reasoning, so the split marker is never reassembled and the answer stays in reasoning_text.
Harness flags:
Parity harness flags used for this result:
dynamo: parser_family=deepseek_r1; in_reasoning=false; token_chunks=none
vllm: reasoning_parser=deepseek_r1; chat_template_kwargs={}; delta_token_ids=derived from stub tokenizer
sglang: model_type=deepseek-r1; stream_reasoning=true; force_reasoning=false

Not set by this parser-level parity harness:
- frontend `tool_choice`
- SGLang `separate_reasoning`
- request `enable_thinking` / `thinking` / `thinking_mode` unless shown in vLLM chat_template_kwargs above

inspired by vLLM DeepSeek R1 reasoning tests: https://github.com/vllm-project/vllm/blob/39910f2b25aacc09f5e7f166cdf0030b19f8b9e8/tests/reasoning/test_deepseekr1_reasoning_parser.py; local taxonomy: lib/parsers/REASONING_CASES.md

lib/parsers/REASONING_CASES.md; https://docs.nvidia.com/dynamo/dev/user-guides/reasoning/reasoning-parsing-dynamo

Legend: = all captured peers match Dynamo · D Dynamo-only fixture (both peers unavailable) · V/S divergence (V = vLLM, S = SGLang; intentional, has reason:) · ? more research needed (e.g. V?, S? — diverges with no reason: yet) · ↯ Dynamo leaks reasoning markup or final-answer text · ! expected-error suffix (e.g. V!, S! — engine crashes by design) · n/a not applicable.
† = no vLLM peer reasoning parser for this family · § = no SGLang peer reasoning parser for this family.

Tooltip fields: input_text=raw model output or stream chunks fed into the reasoning parser · reasoning_text=hidden reasoning content extracted by the parser · normal_text=residual text passed onward to response assembly or downstream parsers · harness flags=the exact parser-level arguments used for the parity result.

Omitted tool calling parser rows: no corresponding Dynamo reasoning parser fixture for AI21 Jamba (jamba), Hermes-3 / Llama variants (hermes), Llama 3 (JSON fmt) (llama3_json), Llama 4 (pythonic fmt) (pythonic), Phi-4 (phi4), Qwen 2.5 (qwen25).

Stats: 15 families × 10 sub-cases = 150 grid slots (42 n/a, 0 missing). 108 real cases: 41 captured-peer parity · 0 Dynamo-only · 58 documented divergences (have reason:) · 9 research-needed (no reason: yet) · 0 expected-errors.

Case descriptions

Full case definitions: lib/parsers/REASONING_CASES.md.

Core
REASONING.stream.1.aEmpty stream chunk — no emitted content. Parser must not crash, buffer forever, or invent reasoning text
REASONING.stream.1.bPlain text stream, no reasoning markers — chunks contain user-visible text only. Explicit-marker parsers should pass it through as `normal_text`; force-reasoning parsers may keep it in `reasoning_text`
Reasoning extraction
REASONING.stream.2.aSingle reasoning block across N chunks — incremental assembly of `<think>...</think>` content over multiple chunks of any sizing
Multi-span
REASONING.stream.2.bMultiple reasoning spans across chunks — same contract as `REASONING.batch.6.*`, but state must reset between spans
Chunk boundaries
REASONING.stream.3.aStart-marker chunk-boundary split — opening `<think>` (or analog) straddles a chunk boundary; partial-token matching must keep buffering instead of flushing as plain text
REASONING.stream.3.bEnd-marker chunk-boundary split — closing `</think>` straddles a chunk boundary; same buffering contract as `REASONING.stream.3.a`
REASONING.stream.3.cPartial marker prefix later proves not to be a marker — emit the buffered text according to the parser's current state
Other
REASONING.stream.4.a
REASONING.stream.4.b
REASONING.stream.4.c
